Come out and celebrate with Sammy Kershaw (Third Rate Romance, Yardsale, Queen of My Double Wide Trailer), Aaron Tippin (You ve Got To Stand For Something, Workin Mans Ph.D, Blue Angel) and Collin Raye (The Verge, I Want You Bad (And That Aint Good), My Kind Of Girl). Each artist will sing acoustic versions of the songs that gave them their top successes!
